\DoxyCodeLine{24 \textcolor{comment}{ * If you wish an application built against the newest version of DirectDraw}}
\DoxyCodeLine{25 \textcolor{comment}{ * to run against an older DirectDraw run time then define DIRECTDRAW\_VERSION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{26 \textcolor{comment}{ * to be the earlies version of DirectDraw you wish to run against. For,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{27 \textcolor{comment}{ * example if you wish an application to run against a DX 3 runtime define}}
\DoxyCodeLine{28 \textcolor{comment}{ * DIRECTDRAW\_VERSION to be 0x0300.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{29 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{177 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{178 \textcolor{comment}{ * Flags for DirectDrawEnumerateEx}}
\DoxyCodeLine{179 \textcolor{comment}{ * DirectDrawEnumerateEx supercedes DirectDrawEnumerate. You must use GetProcAddress to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{180 \textcolor{comment}{ * obtain a function pointer (of type LPDIRECTDRAWENUMERATEEX) to DirectDrawEnumerateEx.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{181 \textcolor{comment}{ * By default, only the primary display device is enumerated.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{182 \textcolor{comment}{ * DirectDrawEnumerate is equivalent to DirectDrawEnumerate(,,DDENUM\_NONDISPLAYDEVICES)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{183 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{184 }

\DoxyCodeLine{188 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{189 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDENUM\_ATTACHEDSECONDARYDEVICES     0x00000001L}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2522 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2523 \textcolor{comment}{/*============================================================================}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2524 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2525 \textcolor{comment}{ * Direct Draw Capability Flags}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2526 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2527 \textcolor{comment}{ * These flags are used to describe the capabilities of a given Surface.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2528 \textcolor{comment}{ * All flags are bit flags.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2529 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2530 \textcolor{comment}{ *==========================================================================*/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2531 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2532 \textcolor{comment}{/****************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2533 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2534 \textcolor{comment}{ * DIRECTDRAWSURFACE CAPABILITY FLAGS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2535 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2536 \textcolor{comment}{ ****************************************************************************/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2537 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2538 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2539 \textcolor{comment}{ * This bit is reserved. It should not be specified.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2540 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2541 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDSCAPS\_RESERVED1                       0x00000001l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2542 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2543 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2544 \textcolor{comment}{ * Indicates that this surface contains alpha-\/only information.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2545 \textcolor{comment}{ * (To determine if a surface is RGBA/YUVA, the pixel format must be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2546 \textcolor{comment}{ * interrogated.)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2547 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2548 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDSCAPS\_ALPHA                           0x00000002l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2549 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2550 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2551 \textcolor{comment}{ * Indicates that this surface is a backbuffer.  It is generally}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2552 \textcolor{comment}{ * set by CreateSurface when the DDSCAPS\_FLIP capability bit is set.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2553 \textcolor{comment}{ * It indicates that this surface is THE back buffer of a surface}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2554 \textcolor{comment}{ * flipping structure.  DirectDraw supports N surfaces in a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2555 \textcolor{comment}{ * surface flipping structure.  Only the surface that immediately}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2556 \textcolor{comment}{ * precedeces the DDSCAPS\_FRONTBUFFER has this capability bit set.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2557 \textcolor{comment}{ * The other surfaces are identified as back buffers by the presence}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2558 \textcolor{comment}{ * of the DDSCAPS\_FLIP capability, their attachment order, and the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2559 \textcolor{comment}{ * absence of the DDSCAPS\_FRONTBUFFER and DDSCAPS\_BACKBUFFER}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2560 \textcolor{comment}{ * capabilities.  The bit is sent to CreateSurface when a standalone}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2561 \textcolor{comment}{ * back buffer is being created.  This surface could be attached to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2562 \textcolor{comment}{ * a front buffer and/or back buffers to form a flipping surface}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2563 \textcolor{comment}{ * structure after the CreateSurface call.  See AddAttachments for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2564 \textcolor{comment}{ * a detailed description of the behaviors in this case.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2565 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2566 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDSCAPS\_BACKBUFFER                      0x00000004l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2567 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2568 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2569 \textcolor{comment}{ * Indicates a complex surface structure is being described.  A}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2570 \textcolor{comment}{ * complex surface structure results in the creation of more than}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2571 \textcolor{comment}{ * one surface.  The additional surfaces are attached to the root}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2572 \textcolor{comment}{ * surface.  The complex structure can only be destroyed by}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2573 \textcolor{comment}{ * destroying the root.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2574 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2575 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDSCAPS\_COMPLEX                         0x00000008l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2576 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2577 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2578 \textcolor{comment}{ * Indicates that this surface is a part of a surface flipping structure.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2579 \textcolor{comment}{ * When it is passed to CreateSurface the DDSCAPS\_FRONTBUFFER and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2580 \textcolor{comment}{ * DDSCAP\_BACKBUFFER bits are not set.  They are set by CreateSurface}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2581 \textcolor{comment}{ * on the resulting creations.  The dwBackBufferCount field in the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2582 \textcolor{comment}{ * DDSURFACEDESC structure must be set to at least 1 in order for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2583 \textcolor{comment}{ * the CreateSurface call to succeed.  The DDSCAPS\_COMPLEX capability}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2584 \textcolor{comment}{ * must always be set with creating multiple surfaces through CreateSurface.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2585 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2586 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDSCAPS\_FLIP                            0x00000010l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2587 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2588 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2589 \textcolor{comment}{ * Indicates that this surface is THE front buffer of a surface flipping}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2590 \textcolor{comment}{ * structure.  It is generally set by CreateSurface when the DDSCAPS\_FLIP}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2591 \textcolor{comment}{ * capability bit is set.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2592 \textcolor{comment}{ * If this capability is sent to CreateSurface then a standalonw front buffer}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2593 \textcolor{comment}{ * is created.  This surface will not have the DDSCAPS\_FLIP capability.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2594 \textcolor{comment}{ * It can be attached to other back buffers to form a flipping structure.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2595 \textcolor{comment}{ * See AddAttachments for a detailed description of the behaviors in this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2596 \textcolor{comment}{ * case.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2597 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2598 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDSCAPS\_FRONTBUFFER                     0x00000020l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2599 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2600 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2601 \textcolor{comment}{ * Indicates that this surface is any offscreen surface that is not an overlay,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2602 \textcolor{comment}{ * texture, zbuffer, front buffer, back buffer, or alpha surface.  It is used}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2603 \textcolor{comment}{ * to identify plain vanilla surfaces.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2604 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2605 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDSCAPS\_OFFSCREENPLAIN                  0x00000040l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2606 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2607 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2608 \textcolor{comment}{ * Indicates that this surface is an overlay.  It may or may not be directly visible}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2609 \textcolor{comment}{ * depending on whether or not it is currently being overlayed onto the primary}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2610 \textcolor{comment}{ * surface.  DDSCAPS\_VISIBLE can be used to determine whether or not it is being}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2611 \textcolor{comment}{ * overlayed at the moment.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2612 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2613 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDSCAPS\_OVERLAY                         0x00000080l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2614 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2615 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2616 \textcolor{comment}{ * Indicates that unique DirectDrawPalette objects can be created and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2617 \textcolor{comment}{ * attached to this surface.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2618 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2619 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDSCAPS\_PALETTE                         0x00000100l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2620 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2621 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2622 \textcolor{comment}{ * Indicates that this surface is the primary surface.  The primary}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2623 \textcolor{comment}{ * surface represents what the user is seeing at the moment.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2624 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2625 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDSCAPS\_PRIMARYSURFACE                  0x00000200l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2626 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2627 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2628 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2629 \textcolor{comment}{ * This flag used to be DDSCAPS\_PRIMARYSURFACELEFT, which is now}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2630 \textcolor{comment}{ * obsolete.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2631 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2632 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDSCAPS\_RESERVED3               0x00000400l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2633 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDSCAPS\_PRIMARYSURFACELEFT              0x00000000l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2634 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2635 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2636 \textcolor{comment}{ * Indicates that this surface memory was allocated in system memory}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2637 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2638 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDSCAPS\_SYSTEMMEMORY                    0x00000800l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2639 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2640 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2641 \textcolor{comment}{ * Indicates that this surface can be used as a 3D texture.  It does not}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2642 \textcolor{comment}{ * indicate whether or not the surface is being used for that purpose.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2643 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2644 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDSCAPS\_TEXTURE                         0x00001000l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2645 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2646 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2647 \textcolor{comment}{ * Indicates that a surface may be a destination for 3D rendering.  This}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2648 \textcolor{comment}{ * bit must be set in order to query for a Direct3D Device Interface}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2649 \textcolor{comment}{ * from this surface.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2650 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2651 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDSCAPS\_3DDEVICE                        0x00002000l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2652 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2653 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2655 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2656 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDSCAPS\_VIDEOMEMORY                     0x00004000l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2657 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2658 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2659 \textcolor{comment}{ * Indicates that changes made to this surface are immediately visible.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2660 \textcolor{comment}{ * It is always set for the primary surface and is set for overlays while}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2661 \textcolor{comment}{ * they are being overlayed and texture maps while they are being textured.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2662 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2663 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDSCAPS\_VISIBLE                         0x00008000l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2664 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2665 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2666 \textcolor{comment}{ * Indicates that only writes are permitted to the surface.  Read accesses}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2667 \textcolor{comment}{ * from the surface may or may not generate a protection fault, but the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2668 \textcolor{comment}{ * results of a read from this surface will not be meaningful.  READ ONLY.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2669 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2670 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDSCAPS\_WRITEONLY                       0x00010000l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2671 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2672 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2673 \textcolor{comment}{ * Indicates that this surface is a z buffer. A z buffer does not contain}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2674 \textcolor{comment}{ * displayable information.  Instead it contains bit depth information that is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2675 \textcolor{comment}{ * used to determine which pixels are visible and which are obscured.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2676 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2677 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDSCAPS\_ZBUFFER                         0x00020000l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2678 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2679 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2680 \textcolor{comment}{ * Indicates surface will have a DC associated long term}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2681 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2682 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDSCAPS\_OWNDC                           0x00040000l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2683 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2684 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2685 \textcolor{comment}{ * Indicates surface should be able to receive live video}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2686 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2687 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDSCAPS\_LIVEVIDEO                       0x00080000l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2688 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2689 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2690 \textcolor{comment}{ * Indicates surface should be able to have a stream decompressed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2691 \textcolor{comment}{ * to it by the hardware.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2692 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2693 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDSCAPS\_HWCODEC                         0x00100000l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2694 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2695 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2696 \textcolor{comment}{ * Surface is a ModeX surface.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2697 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2698 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2699 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDSCAPS\_MODEX                           0x00200000l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2700 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2701 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2702 \textcolor{comment}{ * Indicates surface is one level of a mip-\/map. This surface will}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2703 \textcolor{comment}{ * be attached to other DDSCAPS\_MIPMAP surfaces to form the mip-\/map.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2704 \textcolor{comment}{ * This can be done explicitly, by creating a number of surfaces and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2705 \textcolor{comment}{ * attaching them with AddAttachedSurface or by implicitly by CreateSurface.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2706 \textcolor{comment}{ * If this bit is set then DDSCAPS\_TEXTURE must also be set.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2707 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2708 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDSCAPS\_MIPMAP                          0x00400000l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2709 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2710 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2711 \textcolor{comment}{ * This bit is reserved. It should not be specified.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2712 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2713 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDSCAPS\_RESERVED2                       0x00800000l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2714 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2715 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2716 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2717 \textcolor{comment}{ * Indicates that memory for the surface is not allocated until the surface}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2718 \textcolor{comment}{ * is loaded (via the Direct3D texture Load() function).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2719 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2720 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDSCAPS\_ALLOCONLOAD                     0x04000000l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2721 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2722 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2723 \textcolor{comment}{ * Indicates that the surface will recieve data from a video port.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2724 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2725 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDSCAPS\_VIDEOPORT                       0x08000000l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2726 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2727 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2728 \textcolor{comment}{ * Indicates that a video memory surface is resident in true, local video}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2729 \textcolor{comment}{ * memory rather than non-\/local video memory. If this flag is specified then}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2730 \textcolor{comment}{ * so must DDSCAPS\_VIDEOMEMORY. This flag is mutually exclusive with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2731 \textcolor{comment}{ * DDSCAPS\_NONLOCALVIDMEM.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2732 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2733 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDSCAPS\_LOCALVIDMEM                     0x10000000l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2734 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2735 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2736 \textcolor{comment}{ * Indicates that a video memory surface is resident in non-\/local video}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2737 \textcolor{comment}{ * memory rather than true, local video memory. If this flag is specified}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2738 \textcolor{comment}{ * then so must DDSCAPS\_VIDEOMEMORY. This flag is mutually exclusive with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2739 \textcolor{comment}{ * DDSCAPS\_LOCALVIDMEM.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2740 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2741 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDSCAPS\_NONLOCALVIDMEM                  0x20000000l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2742 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2743 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2744 \textcolor{comment}{ * Indicates that this surface is a standard VGA mode surface, and not a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2745 \textcolor{comment}{ * ModeX surface. (This flag will never be set in combination with the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2746 \textcolor{comment}{ * DDSCAPS\_MODEX flag).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2747 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2748 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDSCAPS\_STANDARDVGAMODE                 0x40000000l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2749 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2750 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2751 \textcolor{comment}{ * Indicates that this surface will be an optimized surface. This flag is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2752 \textcolor{comment}{ * currently only valid in conjunction with the DDSCAPS\_TEXTURE flag. The surface}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2753 \textcolor{comment}{ * will be created without any underlying video memory until loaded.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2754 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2755 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDSCAPS\_OPTIMIZED                       0x80000000l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2756 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2757 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2758 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2759 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2760 \textcolor{comment}{ * This bit is reserved}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2761 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2762 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDSCAPS2\_RESERVED4                      0x00000002L}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2763 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDSCAPS2\_HARDWAREDEINTERLACE            0x00000000L}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2764 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2765 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2766 \textcolor{comment}{ * Indicates to the driver that this surface will be locked very frequently}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2767 \textcolor{comment}{ * (for procedural textures, dynamic lightmaps, etc). Surfaces with this cap}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2768 \textcolor{comment}{ * set must also have DDSCAPS\_TEXTURE. This cap cannot be used with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2769 \textcolor{comment}{ * DDSCAPS2\_HINTSTATIC and DDSCAPS2\_OPAQUE.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2770 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2771 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDSCAPS2\_HINTDYNAMIC                    0x00000004L}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2772 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2773 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2774 \textcolor{comment}{ * Indicates to the driver that this surface can be re-\/ordered/retiled on}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2775 \textcolor{comment}{ * load. This operation will not change the size of the texture. It is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2776 \textcolor{comment}{ * relatively fast and symmetrical, since the application may lock these}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2777 \textcolor{comment}{ * bits (although it will take a performance hit when doing so). Surfaces}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2778 \textcolor{comment}{ * with this cap set must also have DDSCAPS\_TEXTURE. This cap cannot be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2779 \textcolor{comment}{ * used with DDSCAPS2\_HINTDYNAMIC and DDSCAPS2\_OPAQUE.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2780 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2781 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDSCAPS2\_HINTSTATIC                     0x00000008L}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2782 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2783 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2784 \textcolor{comment}{ * Indicates that the client would like this texture surface to be managed by the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2785 \textcolor{comment}{ * DirectDraw/Direct3D runtime. Surfaces with this cap set must also have}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2786 \textcolor{comment}{ * DDSCAPS\_TEXTURE set.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2787 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2788 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDSCAPS2\_TEXTUREMANAGE                  0x00000010L}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2789 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2790 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2791 \textcolor{comment}{ * These bits are reserved for internal use */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2792 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDSCAPS2\_RESERVED1                      0x00000020L}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2793 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDSCAPS2\_RESERVED2                      0x00000040L}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2794 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2795 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2796 \textcolor{comment}{ * Indicates to the driver that this surface will never be locked again.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2797 \textcolor{comment}{ * The driver is free to optimize this surface via retiling and actual compression.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2798 \textcolor{comment}{ * All calls to Lock() or Blts from this surface will fail. Surfaces with this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2799 \textcolor{comment}{ * cap set must also have DDSCAPS\_TEXTURE. This cap cannot be used with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2800 \textcolor{comment}{ * DDSCAPS2\_HINTDYNAMIC and DDSCAPS2\_HINTSTATIC.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2801 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2802 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDSCAPS2\_OPAQUE                         0x00000080L}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2803 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2804 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2805 \textcolor{comment}{ * Applications should set this bit at CreateSurface time to indicate that they}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2806 \textcolor{comment}{ * intend to use antialiasing. Only valid if DDSCAPS\_3DDEVICE is also set.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2807 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2808 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDSCAPS2\_HINTANTIALIASING               0x00000100L}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2809 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2810 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2811 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2812 \textcolor{comment}{ * This flag is used at CreateSurface time to indicate that this set of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2813 \textcolor{comment}{ * surfaces is a cubic environment map}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2814 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2815 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDSCAPS2\_CUBEMAP                        0x00000200L}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2816 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2817 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2818 \textcolor{comment}{ * These flags preform two functions:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2819 \textcolor{comment}{ * -\/ At CreateSurface time, they define which of the six cube faces are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2820 \textcolor{comment}{ *   required by the application.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2821 \textcolor{comment}{ * -\/ After creation, each face in the cubemap will have exactly one of these}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2822 \textcolor{comment}{ *   bits set.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2823 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2824 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDSCAPS2\_CUBEMAP\_POSITIVEX              0x00000400L}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2825 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDSCAPS2\_CUBEMAP\_NEGATIVEX              0x00000800L}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2826 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDSCAPS2\_CUBEMAP\_POSITIVEY              0x00001000L}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2827 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDSCAPS2\_CUBEMAP\_NEGATIVEY              0x00002000L}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2828 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDSCAPS2\_CUBEMAP\_POSITIVEZ              0x00004000L}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2829 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDSCAPS2\_CUBEMAP\_NEGATIVEZ              0x00008000L}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2830 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2831 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2832 \textcolor{comment}{ * This macro may be used to specify all faces of a cube map at CreateSurface time}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2833 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2834 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDSCAPS2\_CUBEMAP\_ALLFACES ( DDSCAPS2\_CUBEMAP\_POSITIVEX |\(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2835 \textcolor{preprocessor}{                                    DDSCAPS2\_CUBEMAP\_NEGATIVEX |\(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2836 \textcolor{preprocessor}{                                    DDSCAPS2\_CUBEMAP\_POSITIVEY |\(\backslash\)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2840 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2841 }

\DoxyCodeLine{2845 \textcolor{comment}{ * constructs such as Cube Maps, wherein there are more than one mipmap surface attached}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2859 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2860 }

\DoxyCodeLine{2900 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2901 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2902 \textcolor{comment}{ * Indicates that all surfaces in this creation chain should be given an alpha channel.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2903 \textcolor{comment}{ * This flag will be set on primary surface chains that may have no explicit pixel format}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2904 \textcolor{comment}{ * (and thus take on the format of the current display mode).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2905 \textcolor{comment}{ * The driver should infer that all these surfaces have a format having an alpha channel.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2906 \textcolor{comment}{ * (e.g. assume D3DFMT\_A8R8G8B8 if the display mode is x888.)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2907 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2908 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDSCAPS2\_ENABLEALPHACHANNEL             0x20000000L}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2909 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2910 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2911 \textcolor{comment}{ * Indicates that all surfaces in this creation chain is extended primary surface format.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2912 \textcolor{comment}{ * This flag will be set on extended primary surface chains that always have explicit pixel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2913 \textcolor{comment}{ * format and the pixel format is typically GDI (Graphics Device Interface) couldn't handle,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2914 \textcolor{comment}{ * thus only used with fullscreen application. (e.g. D3DFMT\_A2R10G10B10 format)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2915 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2916 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDSCAPS2\_EXTENDEDFORMATPRIMARY          0x40000000L}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2917 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2918 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2919 \textcolor{comment}{ * Indicates that all surfaces in this creation chain is additional primary surface.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2920 \textcolor{comment}{ * This flag will be set on primary surface chains which must present on the adapter}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2921 \textcolor{comment}{ * id provided on dwCaps4. Typically this will be used to create secondary primary surface}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2922 \textcolor{comment}{ * on DualView display adapter.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2923 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2924 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDSCAPS2\_ADDITIONALPRIMARY              0x80000000L}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2925 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2926 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2929 \textcolor{comment}{ * when multisampling}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2930 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2937 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2973 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2974 \textcolor{comment}{ * Display hardware has 3D acceleration.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2975 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2977 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2978 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2979 \textcolor{comment}{ * Indicates that DirectDraw will support only dest rectangles that are aligned}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2980 \textcolor{comment}{ * on DIRECTDRAWCAPS.dwAlignBoundaryDest boundaries of the surface, respectively.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2981 \textcolor{comment}{ * READ ONLY.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2982 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2983 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDCAPS\_ALIGNBOUNDARYDEST        0x00000002l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2984 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2985 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2986 \textcolor{comment}{ * Indicates that DirectDraw will support only source rectangles  whose sizes in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2987 \textcolor{comment}{ * BYTEs are DIRECTDRAWCAPS.dwAlignSizeDest multiples, respectively.  READ ONLY.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2988 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2989 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDCAPS\_ALIGNSIZEDEST            0x00000004l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2990 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2991 \textcolor{comment}{ * Indicates that DirectDraw will support only source rectangles that are aligned}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2992 \textcolor{comment}{ * on DIRECTDRAWCAPS.dwAlignBoundarySrc boundaries of the surface, respectively.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2993 \textcolor{comment}{ * READ ONLY.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2994 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2995 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDCAPS\_ALIGNBOUNDARYSRC         0x00000008l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2996 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2997 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2998 \textcolor{comment}{ * Indicates that DirectDraw will support only source rectangles  whose sizes in}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3000 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3001 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDCAPS\_ALIGNSIZESRC             0x00000010l}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3008 }

\DoxyCodeLine{3146 \textcolor{comment}{ * MORE DIRECTDRAW DRIVER CAPABILITY FLAGS (dwCaps2)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3148 \textcolor{comment}{ ****************************************************************************/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3149 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3150 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3151 \textcolor{comment}{ * Display hardware is certified}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3152 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3153 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDCAPS2\_CERTIFIED              0x00000001l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3154 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3155 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3156 \textcolor{comment}{ * Driver cannot interleave 2D operations (lock and blt) to surfaces with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3157 \textcolor{comment}{ * Direct3D rendering operations between calls to BeginScene() and EndScene()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3158 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3159 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDCAPS2\_NO2DDURING3DSCENE       0x00000002l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3160 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3161 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3162 \textcolor{comment}{ * Display hardware contains a video port}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3163 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3164 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDCAPS2\_VIDEOPORT               0x00000004l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3165 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3166 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3167 \textcolor{comment}{ * The overlay can be automatically flipped according to the video port}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3168 \textcolor{comment}{ * VSYNCs, providing automatic doubled buffered display of video port}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3169 \textcolor{comment}{ * data using an overlay}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3170 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3171 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDCAPS2\_AUTOFLIPOVERLAY         0x00000008l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3172 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3173 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3174 \textcolor{comment}{ * Overlay can display each field of interlaced data individually while}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3175 \textcolor{comment}{ * it is interleaved in memory without causing jittery artifacts.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3176 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3177 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDCAPS2\_CANBOBINTERLEAVED       0x00000010l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3178 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3179 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3180 \textcolor{comment}{ * Overlay can display each field of interlaced data individually while}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3181 \textcolor{comment}{ * it is not interleaved in memory without causing jittery artifacts.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3182 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3183 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDCAPS2\_CANBOBNONINTERLEAVED    0x00000020l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3184 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3185 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3186 \textcolor{comment}{ * The overlay surface contains color controls (brightness, sharpness, etc.)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3187 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3188 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDCAPS2\_COLORCONTROLOVERLAY     0x00000040l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3189 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3190 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3191 \textcolor{comment}{ * The primary surface contains color controls (gamma, etc.)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3192 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3193 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDCAPS2\_COLORCONTROLPRIMARY     0x00000080l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3194 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3195 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3196 \textcolor{comment}{ * RGBZ -\/> RGB supported for 16:16 RGB:Z}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3197 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3198 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDCAPS2\_CANDROPZ16BIT           0x00000100l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3199 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3200 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3201 \textcolor{comment}{ * Driver supports non-\/local video memory.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3202 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3203 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDCAPS2\_NONLOCALVIDMEM          0x00000200l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3204 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3205 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3206 \textcolor{comment}{ * Dirver supports non-\/local video memory but has different capabilities for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3207 \textcolor{comment}{ * non-\/local video memory surfaces. If this bit is set then so must}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3208 \textcolor{comment}{ * DDCAPS2\_NONLOCALVIDMEM.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3209 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3210 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDCAPS2\_NONLOCALVIDMEMCAPS      0x00000400l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3211 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3212 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3213 \textcolor{comment}{ * Driver neither requires nor prefers surfaces to be pagelocked when performing}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3214 \textcolor{comment}{ * blts involving system memory surfaces}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3215 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3216 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDCAPS2\_NOPAGELOCKREQUIRED      0x00000800l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3217 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3218 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3219 \textcolor{comment}{ * Driver can create surfaces which are wider than the primary surface}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3220 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3221 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDCAPS2\_WIDESURFACES            0x00001000l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3222 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3223 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3224 \textcolor{comment}{ * Driver supports bob without using a video port by handling the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3225 \textcolor{comment}{ * DDFLIP\_ODD and DDFLIP\_EVEN flags specified in Flip.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3226 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3227 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDCAPS2\_CANFLIPODDEVEN          0x00002000l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3228 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3229 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3230 \textcolor{comment}{ * Driver supports bob using hardware}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3231 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3232 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDCAPS2\_CANBOBHARDWARE          0x00004000l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3233 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3234 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3235 \textcolor{comment}{ * Driver supports bltting any FOURCC surface to another surface of the same FOURCC}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3236 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3237 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDCAPS2\_COPYFOURCC              0x00008000l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3238 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3239 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3240 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3241 \textcolor{comment}{ * Driver supports loadable gamma ramps for the primary surface}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3242 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3243 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDCAPS2\_PRIMARYGAMMA            0x00020000l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3244 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3245 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3246 \textcolor{comment}{ * Driver can render in windowed mode.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3247 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3248 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDCAPS2\_CANRENDERWINDOWED       0x00080000l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3249 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3250 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3251 \textcolor{comment}{ * A calibrator is available to adjust the gamma ramp according to the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3252 \textcolor{comment}{ * physical display properties so that the result will be identical on}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3253 \textcolor{comment}{ * all calibrated systems.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3254 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3255 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDCAPS2\_CANCALIBRATEGAMMA       0x00100000l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3256 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3257 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3258 \textcolor{comment}{ * Indicates that the driver will respond to DDFLIP\_INTERVALn flags}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3259 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3260 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDCAPS2\_FLIPINTERVAL            0x00200000l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3261 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3262 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3263 \textcolor{comment}{ * Indicates that the driver will respond to DDFLIP\_NOVSYNC}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3264 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3265 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDCAPS2\_FLIPNOVSYNC             0x00400000l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3266 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3267 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3268 \textcolor{comment}{ * Driver supports management of video memory, if this flag is ON,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3269 \textcolor{comment}{ * driver manages the texture if requested with DDSCAPS2\_TEXTUREMANAGE on}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3270 \textcolor{comment}{ * DirectX manages the texture if this flag is OFF and surface has DDSCAPS2\_TEXTUREMANAGE on}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3271 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3272 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDCAPS2\_CANMANAGETEXTURE        0x00800000l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3273 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3274 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3275 \textcolor{comment}{ * The Direct3D texture manager uses this cap to decide whether to put managed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3276 \textcolor{comment}{ * surfaces in non-\/local video memory. If the cap is set, the texture manager will}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3277 \textcolor{comment}{ * put managed surfaces in non-\/local vidmem. Drivers that cannot texture from}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3278 \textcolor{comment}{ * local vidmem SHOULD NOT set this cap.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3279 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3280 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDCAPS2\_TEXMANINNONLOCALVIDMEM  0x01000000l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3281 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3282 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3283 \textcolor{comment}{ * Indicates that the driver supports DX7 type of stereo in at least one mode (which may}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3284 \textcolor{comment}{ * not necessarily be the current mode). Applications should use IDirectDraw7 (or higher)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3285 \textcolor{comment}{ * ::EnumDisplayModes and check the DDSURFACEDESC.ddsCaps.dwCaps2 field for the presence of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3286 \textcolor{comment}{ * DDSCAPS2\_STEREOSURFACELEFT to check if a particular mode supports stereo. The application}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3287 \textcolor{comment}{ * can also use IDirectDraw7(or higher)::GetDisplayMode to check the current mode.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3288 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3289 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDCAPS2\_STEREO                  0x02000000L}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3290 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3291 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3292 \textcolor{comment}{ * This caps bit is intended for internal DirectDraw use.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3293 \textcolor{comment}{ * -\/It is only valid if DDCAPS2\_NONLOCALVIDMEMCAPS is set.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3294 \textcolor{comment}{ * -\/If this bit is set, then DDCAPS\_CANBLTSYSMEM MUST be set by the driver (and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3295 \textcolor{comment}{ *  all the assoicated system memory blt caps must be correct).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3296 \textcolor{comment}{ * -\/It implies that the system-\/>video blt caps in DDCAPS also apply to system to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3297 \textcolor{comment}{ *  nonlocal blts. I.e. the dwSVBCaps, dwSVBCKeyCaps, dwSVBFXCaps and dwSVBRops}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3298 \textcolor{comment}{ *  members of DDCAPS (DDCORECAPS) are filled in correctly.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3299 \textcolor{comment}{ * -\/Any blt from system to nonlocal memory that matches these caps bits will}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3300 \textcolor{comment}{ *  be passed to the driver.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3301 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3302 \textcolor{comment}{ * NOTE: This is intended to enable the driver itself to do efficient reordering}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3303 \textcolor{comment}{ * of textures. This is NOT meant to imply that hardware can write into AGP memory.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3304 \textcolor{comment}{ * This operation is not currently supported.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3305 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3306 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDCAPS2\_SYSTONONLOCAL\_AS\_SYSTOLOCAL   0x04000000L}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3307 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3308 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3309 \textcolor{comment}{ * was DDCAPS2\_PUREHAL}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3310 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3311 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDCAPS2\_RESERVED1                     0x08000000L}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3312 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3313 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3314 \textcolor{comment}{ * Driver supports management of video memory, if this flag is ON,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3315 \textcolor{comment}{ * driver manages the resource if requested with DDSCAPS2\_TEXTUREMANAGE on}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3316 \textcolor{comment}{ * DirectX manages the resource if this flag is OFF and surface has DDSCAPS2\_TEXTUREMANAGE on}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3317 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3318 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDCAPS2\_CANMANAGERESOURCE             0x10000000L}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3319 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3320 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3321 \textcolor{comment}{ * Driver supports dynamic textures. This will allow the application to set}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3322 \textcolor{comment}{ * D3DUSAGE\_DYNAMIC (DDSCAPS2\_HINTDYNAMIC for drivers) at texture create time.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3323 \textcolor{comment}{ * Video memory dynamic textures WILL be lockable by applications. It is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3324 \textcolor{comment}{ * expected that these locks will be very efficient (which implies that the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3325 \textcolor{comment}{ * driver should always maintain a linear copy, a pointer to which can be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3326 \textcolor{comment}{ * quickly handed out to the application).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3327 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3328 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDCAPS2\_DYNAMICTEXTURES               0x20000000L}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3329 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3330 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3331 \textcolor{comment}{ * Driver supports auto-\/generation of mipmaps.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3332 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3333 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDCAPS2\_CANAUTOGENMIPMAP              0x40000000L}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3341 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3342 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3343 \textcolor{comment}{ * Supports alpha blending around the edge of a source color keyed surface.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3344 \textcolor{comment}{ * For Blt.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3345 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3346 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDFXALPHACAPS\_BLTALPHAEDGEBLEND         0x00000001l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3347 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3348 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3349 \textcolor{comment}{ * Supports alpha information in the pixel format.  The bit depth of alpha}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3350 \textcolor{comment}{ * information in the pixel format can be 1,2,4, or 8.  The alpha value becomes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3351 \textcolor{comment}{ * more opaque as the alpha value increases.  (0 is transparent.)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3352 \textcolor{comment}{ * For Blt.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3353 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3354 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDFXALPHACAPS\_BLTALPHAPIXELS            0x00000002l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3355 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3356 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3357 \textcolor{comment}{ * Supports alpha information in the pixel format.  The bit depth of alpha}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3358 \textcolor{comment}{ * information in the pixel format can be 1,2,4, or 8.  The alpha value}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3359 \textcolor{comment}{ * becomes more transparent as the alpha value increases.  (0 is opaque.)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3360 \textcolor{comment}{ * This flag can only be set if DDCAPS\_ALPHA is set.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3361 \textcolor{comment}{ * For Blt.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3362 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3363 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDFXALPHACAPS\_BLTALPHAPIXELSNEG         0x00000004l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3364 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3365 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3366 \textcolor{comment}{ * Supports alpha only surfaces.  The bit depth of an alpha only surface can be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3367 \textcolor{comment}{ * 1,2,4, or 8.  The alpha value becomes more opaque as the alpha value increases.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3368 \textcolor{comment}{ * (0 is transparent.)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3369 \textcolor{comment}{ * For Blt.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3370 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3371 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDFXALPHACAPS\_BLTALPHASURFACES          0x00000008l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3372 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3373 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3374 \textcolor{comment}{ * The depth of the alpha channel data can range can be 1,2,4, or 8.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3375 \textcolor{comment}{ * The NEG suffix indicates that this alpha channel becomes more transparent}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3376 \textcolor{comment}{ * as the alpha value increases. (0 is opaque.)  This flag can only be set if}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3377 \textcolor{comment}{ * DDCAPS\_ALPHA is set.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3378 \textcolor{comment}{ * For Blt.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3379 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3380 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDFXALPHACAPS\_BLTALPHASURFACESNEG       0x00000010l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3381 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3382 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3383 \textcolor{comment}{ * Supports alpha blending around the edge of a source color keyed surface.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3384 \textcolor{comment}{ * For Overlays.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3385 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3386 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDFXALPHACAPS\_OVERLAYALPHAEDGEBLEND     0x00000020l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3387 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3388 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3389 \textcolor{comment}{ * Supports alpha information in the pixel format.  The bit depth of alpha}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3390 \textcolor{comment}{ * information in the pixel format can be 1,2,4, or 8.  The alpha value becomes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3391 \textcolor{comment}{ * more opaque as the alpha value increases.  (0 is transparent.)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3392 \textcolor{comment}{ * For Overlays.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3393 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3394 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDFXALPHACAPS\_OVERLAYALPHAPIXELS        0x00000040l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3395 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3396 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3397 \textcolor{comment}{ * Supports alpha information in the pixel format.  The bit depth of alpha}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3399 \textcolor{comment}{ * becomes more transparent as the alpha value increases.  (0 is opaque.)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3400 \textcolor{comment}{ * This flag can only be set if DDCAPS\_ALPHA is set.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3401 \textcolor{comment}{ * For Overlays.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3402 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3403 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDFXALPHACAPS\_OVERLAYALPHAPIXELSNEG     0x00000080l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3404 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3405 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3409 \textcolor{comment}{ * For Overlays.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3410 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3411 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDFXALPHACAPS\_OVERLAYALPHASURFACES      0x00000100l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3412 }

\DoxyCodeLine{3432 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3433 \textcolor{comment}{ * Uses arithmetic operations to stretch and shrink surfaces during blt}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3434 \textcolor{comment}{ * rather than pixel doubling techniques.  Along the Y axis.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3435 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3436 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDFXCAPS\_BLTARITHSTRETCHY       0x00000020l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3437 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3438 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3439 \textcolor{comment}{ * Uses arithmetic operations to stretch during blt}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3440 \textcolor{comment}{ * rather than pixel doubling techniques.  Along the Y axis. Only}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3441 \textcolor{comment}{ * works for x1, x2, etc.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3442 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3443 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDFXCAPS\_BLTARITHSTRETCHYN      0x00000010l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3444 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3445 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3446 \textcolor{comment}{ * Supports mirroring left to right in blt.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3447 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3448 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDFXCAPS\_BLTMIRRORLEFTRIGHT     0x00000040l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3449 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3450 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3451 \textcolor{comment}{ * Supports mirroring top to bottom in blt.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3452 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3453 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDFXCAPS\_BLTMIRRORUPDOWN        0x00000080l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3454 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3455 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3456 \textcolor{comment}{ * Supports arbitrary rotation for blts.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3457 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3458 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDFXCAPS\_BLTROTATION            0x00000100l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3459 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3460 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3461 \textcolor{comment}{ * Supports 90 degree rotations for blts.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3462 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3463 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDFXCAPS\_BLTROTATION90          0x00000200l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3464 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3465 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3466 \textcolor{comment}{ * DirectDraw supports arbitrary shrinking of a surface along the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3467 \textcolor{comment}{ * x axis (horizontal direction) for blts.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3468 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3469 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDFXCAPS\_BLTSHRINKX             0x00000400l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3470 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3471 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3657 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3658 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3659 \textcolor{comment}{ * Index is onto a 8 bit color index.  This field is only valid with the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3660 \textcolor{comment}{ * DDPCAPS\_1BIT, DDPCAPS\_2BIT or DDPCAPS\_4BIT capability and the target}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3661 \textcolor{comment}{ * surface is in 8bpp. Each color entry is one byte long and is an index}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3662 \textcolor{comment}{ * into destination surface's 8bpp palette.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3663 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3669 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDPCAPS\_8BIT                    0x00000004l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3670 }

\DoxyCodeLine{3674 \textcolor{comment}{ * object.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3675 \textcolor{comment}{ * This flag is obsolete. DirectDraw always initializes the color array from}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3676 \textcolor{comment}{ * the lpDDColorArray parameter. The definition remains for source-\/level}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3677 \textcolor{comment}{ * compatibility.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3678 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3685 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3766 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3767 \textcolor{comment}{ * DIRECTDRAW BITDEPTH CONSTANTS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3768 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3769 \textcolor{comment}{ * NOTE:  These are only used to indicate supported bit depths.   These}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3770 \textcolor{comment}{ * are flags only, they are not to be used as an actual bit depth.   The}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3771 \textcolor{comment}{ * absolute numbers 1, 2, 4, 8, 16, 24 and 32 are used to indicate actual}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3772 \textcolor{comment}{ * bit depths in a surface or for changing the display mode.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3773 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3774 \textcolor{comment}{ ****************************************************************************/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3775 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3776 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3780 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3781 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3782 \textcolor{comment}{ * 2 bits per pixel.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3783 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3784 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDBD\_2                  0x00002000l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3785 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3786 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3787 \textcolor{comment}{ * 4 bits per pixel.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3788 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3789 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDBD\_4                  0x00001000l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3790 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3791 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3792 \textcolor{comment}{ * 8 bits per pixel.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3793 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3794 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDBD\_8                  0x00000800l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3795 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3796 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3797 \textcolor{comment}{ * 16 bits per pixel.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3798 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3799 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDBD\_16                 0x00000400l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3800 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3801 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3802 \textcolor{comment}{ * 24 bits per pixel.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3803 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3804 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDBD\_24                 0X00000200l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3805 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3806 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3808 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3809 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDBD\_32                 0x00000100l}}

\DoxyCodeLine{4192 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4193 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4194 \textcolor{comment}{ * this window will receive the focus messages}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4195 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4196 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDSCL\_SETFOCUSWINDOW                    0x00000080l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4197 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4198 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4199 \textcolor{comment}{ * this window is associated with the DDRAW object and will}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4200 \textcolor{comment}{ * cover the screen in fullscreen mode}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4201 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4202 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDSCL\_SETDEVICEWINDOW                   0x00000100l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4203 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4204 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4205 \textcolor{comment}{ * app wants DDRAW to create a window to be associated with the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4206 \textcolor{comment}{ * DDRAW object}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4207 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4208 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDSCL\_CREATEDEVICEWINDOW                0x00000200l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4209 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4210 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4211 \textcolor{comment}{ * App explicitly asks DDRAW/D3D to be multithread safe. This makes D3D}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4212 \textcolor{comment}{ * take the global crtisec more frequently.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4213 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4214 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDSCL\_MULTITHREADED                     0x00000400l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4215 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4216 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4217 \textcolor{comment}{ * App specifies that it would like to keep the FPU set up for optimal Direct3D}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4218 \textcolor{comment}{ * performance (single precision and exceptions disabled) so Direct3D}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4219 \textcolor{comment}{ * does not need to explicitly set the FPU each time. This is assumed by}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4220 \textcolor{comment}{ * default in DirectX 7. See also DDSCL\_FPUPRESERVE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4221 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4222 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDSCL\_FPUSETUP                          0x00000800l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4223 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4224 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4225 \textcolor{comment}{ * App specifies that it needs either double precision FPU or FPU exceptions}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4226 \textcolor{comment}{ * enabled. This makes Direct3D explicitly set the FPU state eah time it is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4227 \textcolor{comment}{ * called. Setting the flag will reduce Direct3D performance. The flag is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4228 \textcolor{comment}{ * assumed by default in DirectX 6 and earlier. See also DDSCL\_FPUSETUP}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4229 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4230 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDSCL\_FPUPRESERVE                          0x00001000l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4231 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4232 }

\DoxyCodeLine{4321 }

\DoxyCodeLine{4327 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4328 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}

\DoxyCodeLine{4332 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4333 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}

\DoxyCodeLine{4338 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4339 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}

\DoxyCodeLine{4344 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4345 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4346 \textcolor{comment}{ * Use the dwRotationAngle field in the DDBLTFX structure as the angle}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4347 \textcolor{comment}{ * (specified in 1/100th of a degree) to rotate the surface.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4348 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4349 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDBLT\_ROTATIONANGLE                     0x00040000l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4350 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4351 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4352 \textcolor{comment}{ * Z-\/buffered blt using the z-\/buffers attached to the source and destination}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4353 \textcolor{comment}{ * surfaces and the dwZBufferOpCode field in the DDBLTFX structure as the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4354 \textcolor{comment}{ * z-\/buffer opcode.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4355 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4356 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDBLT\_ZBUFFER                           0x00080000l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4357 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4358 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4359 \textcolor{comment}{ * Z-\/buffered blt using the dwConstDest Zfield and the dwZBufferOpCode field}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4360 \textcolor{comment}{ * in the DDBLTFX structure as the z-\/buffer and z-\/buffer opcode respectively}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4361 \textcolor{comment}{ * for the destination.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4362 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4363 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDBLT\_ZBUFFERDESTCONSTOVERRIDE          0x00100000l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4364 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4365 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4366 \textcolor{comment}{ * Z-\/buffered blt using the lpDDSDestZBuffer field and the dwZBufferOpCode}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4367 \textcolor{comment}{ * field in the DDBLTFX structure as the z-\/buffer and z-\/buffer opcode}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4368 \textcolor{comment}{ * respectively for the destination.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4369 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4370 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDBLT\_ZBUFFERDESTOVERRIDE               0x00200000l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4371 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4372 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4373 \textcolor{comment}{ * Z-\/buffered blt using the dwConstSrcZ field and the dwZBufferOpCode field}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4374 \textcolor{comment}{ * in the DDBLTFX structure as the z-\/buffer and z-\/buffer opcode respectively}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4375 \textcolor{comment}{ * for the source.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4376 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4377 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDBLT\_ZBUFFERSRCCONSTOVERRIDE           0x00400000l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4378 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4379 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4380 \textcolor{comment}{ * Z-\/buffered blt using the lpDDSSrcZBuffer field and the dwZBufferOpCode}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4381 \textcolor{comment}{ * field in the DDBLTFX structure as the z-\/buffer and z-\/buffer opcode}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4382 \textcolor{comment}{ * respectively for the source.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4383 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4384 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDBLT\_ZBUFFERSRCOVERRIDE                0x00800000l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4385 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4386 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4387 \textcolor{comment}{ * wait until the device is ready to handle the blt}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4388 \textcolor{comment}{ * this will cause blt to not return DDERR\_WASSTILLDRAWING}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4389 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4390 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDBLT\_WAIT                              0x01000000l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4391 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4392 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4393 \textcolor{comment}{ * Uses the dwFillDepth field in the DDBLTFX structure as the depth value}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4394 \textcolor{comment}{ * to fill the destination rectangle on the destination Z-\/buffer surface}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4395 \textcolor{comment}{ * with.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4396 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4397 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDBLT\_DEPTHFILL                         0x02000000l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4398 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4399 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4400 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4401 \textcolor{comment}{ * Return immediately (with DDERR\_WASSTILLDRAWING) if the device is not}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4402 \textcolor{comment}{ * ready to schedule the blt at the time Blt() is called.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4403 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4404 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDBLT\_DONOTWAIT                         0x08000000l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4405 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4406 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4407 \textcolor{comment}{ * These flags indicate a presentation blt (i.e. a blt}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4408 \textcolor{comment}{ * that moves surface contents from an offscreen back buffer to the primary}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4409 \textcolor{comment}{ * surface). The driver is not allowed to "{}queue"{}  more than three such blts.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4410 \textcolor{comment}{ * The "{}end"{} of the presentation blt is indicated, since the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4411 \textcolor{comment}{ * blt may be clipped, in which case the runtime will call the driver with }}
\DoxyCodeLine{4412 \textcolor{comment}{ * several blts. All blts (even if not clipped) are tagged with DDBLT\_PRESENTATION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4413 \textcolor{comment}{ * and the last (even if not clipped) additionally with DDBLT\_LAST\_PRESENTATION.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4414 \textcolor{comment}{ * Thus the true rule is that the driver must not schedule a DDBLT\_PRESENTATION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4415 \textcolor{comment}{ * blt if there are 3 or more DDBLT\_PRESENTLAST blts in the hardware pipe.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4416 \textcolor{comment}{ * If there are such blts in the pipe, the driver should return DDERR\_WASSTILLDRAWING}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4417 \textcolor{comment}{ * until the oldest queued DDBLT\_LAST\_PRESENTATION blts has been retired (i.e. the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4418 \textcolor{comment}{ * pixels have been actually written to the primary surface). Once the oldest blt}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4419 \textcolor{comment}{ * has been retired, the driver is free to schedule the current blt.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4420 \textcolor{comment}{ * The goal is to provide a mechanism whereby the device's hardware queue never}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4421 \textcolor{comment}{ * gets more than 3 frames ahead of the frames being generated by the application.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4422 \textcolor{comment}{ * When excessive queueing occurs, applications become unusable because the application}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4423 \textcolor{comment}{ * visibly lags user input, and such problems make windowed interactive applications impossible.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4424 \textcolor{comment}{ * Some drivers may not have sufficient knowledge of their hardware's FIFO to know}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4425 \textcolor{comment}{ * when a certain blt has been retired. Such drivers should code cautiously, and }}
\DoxyCodeLine{4426 \textcolor{comment}{ * simply not allow any frames to be queued at all. DDBLT\_LAST\_PRESENTATION should cause}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4427 \textcolor{comment}{ * such drivers to return DDERR\_WASSTILLDRAWING until the accelerator is completely}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4428 \textcolor{comment}{ * finished-\/ exactly as if the application had called Lock on the source surface}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4429 \textcolor{comment}{ * before calling Blt. }}
\DoxyCodeLine{4430 \textcolor{comment}{ * In other words, the driver is allowed and encouraged to }}
\DoxyCodeLine{4431 \textcolor{comment}{ * generate as much latency as it can, but never more than 3 frames worth.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4432 \textcolor{comment}{ * Implementation detail: Drivers should count blts against the SOURCE surface, not}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4433 \textcolor{comment}{ * against the primary surface. This enables multiple parallel windowed application}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4434 \textcolor{comment}{ * to function more optimally.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4435 \textcolor{comment}{ * This flag is passed only to DX8 or higher drivers.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4436 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4437 \textcolor{comment}{ * APPLICATIONS DO NOT SET THESE FLAGS. THEY ARE SET BY THE DIRECTDRAW RUNTIME.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4438 \textcolor{comment}{ * }}
\DoxyCodeLine{4439 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4440 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDBLT\_PRESENTATION                      0x10000000l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4441 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDBLT\_LAST\_PRESENTATION                 0x20000000l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4442 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4443 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4444 \textcolor{comment}{ * If DDBLT\_EXTENDED\_FLAGS is set, then the driver should re-\/interpret}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4445 \textcolor{comment}{ * other flags according to the definitions that follow.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4446 \textcolor{comment}{ * For example, bit 0 (0x00000001L) means DDBLT\_ALPHADEST, unless}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4447 \textcolor{comment}{ * DDBLT\_EXTENDED\_FLAGS is also set, in which case bit 0 means}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4448 \textcolor{comment}{ * DDBLT\_EXTENDED\_LINEAR\_CONTENT.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4449 \textcolor{comment}{ * Only DirectX9 and higher drivers will be given extended blt flags.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4450 \textcolor{comment}{ * Only flags explicitly mentioned here should be re-\/interpreted.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4451 \textcolor{comment}{ * All other flags retain their original meanings.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4452 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4453 \textcolor{comment}{ * List of re-\/interpreted flags:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4454 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4455 \textcolor{comment}{ * Bit Hex value   New meaning                                  old meaning}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4456 \textcolor{comment}{ * -\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4457 \textcolor{comment}{ *  2  0x00000004  DDBLT\_EXTENDED\_LINEAR\_CONTENT                DDBLT\_ALPHADESTNEG}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4458 \textcolor{comment}{ *  4  0x00000010  DDBLT\_EXTENDED\_PRESENTATION\_STRETCHFACTOR    DDBLT\_ALPHAEDGEBLEND}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4459 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4460 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4461 \textcolor{comment}{ * NOTE: APPLICATIONS SHOULD NOT SET THIS FLAG. THIS FLAG IS INTENDED}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4462 \textcolor{comment}{ * FOR USE BY THE DIRECT3D RUNTIME.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4463 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4464 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDBLT\_EXTENDED\_FLAGS                    0x40000000l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4465 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4466 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4467 \textcolor{comment}{ * EXTENDED FLAG. SEE DEFINITION OF DDBLT\_EXTENDED\_FLAGS.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4468 \textcolor{comment}{ * This flag indidcates that the source surface contains content in a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4469 \textcolor{comment}{ * linear color space. The driver may perform gamma correction to the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4470 \textcolor{comment}{ * desktop color space (i.e. sRGB, gamma 2.2) as part of this blt.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4471 \textcolor{comment}{ * If the device can perform such a conversion as part of the copy,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4472 \textcolor{comment}{ * the driver should also set D3DCAPS3\_LINEAR\_TO\_SRGB\_PRESENTATION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4473 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4474 \textcolor{comment}{ * NOTE: APPLICATIONS SHOULD NOT SET THIS FLAG. THIS FLAG IS INTENDED}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4475 \textcolor{comment}{ * FOR USE BY THE DIRECT3D RUNTIME. Use IDirect3DSwapChain9::Present}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4476 \textcolor{comment}{ * and specify D3DPRESENT\_LINEAR\_CONTENT in order to use this functionality.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4477 \textcolor{comment}{ */} }
\DoxyCodeLine{4478 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDBLT\_EXTENDED\_LINEAR\_CONTENT           0x00000004l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4479 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4480 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4481 \textcolor{comment}{/****************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4482 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4483 \textcolor{comment}{ * BLTFAST FLAGS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4484 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4485 \textcolor{comment}{ ****************************************************************************/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4486 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4487 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDBLTFAST\_NOCOLORKEY                    0x00000000}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4488 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDBLTFAST\_SRCCOLORKEY                   0x00000001}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4489 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDBLTFAST\_DESTCOLORKEY                  0x00000002}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4490 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDBLTFAST\_WAIT                          0x00000010}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4491 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDBLTFAST\_DONOTWAIT                     0x00000020}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4492 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4493 \textcolor{comment}{/****************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4494 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4495 \textcolor{comment}{ * FLIP FLAGS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4496 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4497 \textcolor{comment}{ ****************************************************************************/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4498 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4499 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDFLIP\_WAIT                          0x00000001L}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4500 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4501 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4502 \textcolor{comment}{ * Indicates that the target surface contains the even field of video data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4503 \textcolor{comment}{ * This flag is only valid with an overlay surface.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4504 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4505 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDFLIP\_EVEN                          0x00000002L}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4506 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4507 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4508 \textcolor{comment}{ * Indicates that the target surface contains the odd field of video data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4509 \textcolor{comment}{ * This flag is only valid with an overlay surface.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4510 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4511 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDFLIP\_ODD                           0x00000004L}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4512 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4513 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4514 \textcolor{comment}{ * Causes DirectDraw to perform the physical flip immediately and return}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4515 \textcolor{comment}{ * to the application. Typically, what was the front buffer but is now the back}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4516 \textcolor{comment}{ * buffer will still be visible (depending on timing) until the next vertical}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4517 \textcolor{comment}{ * retrace. Subsequent operations involving the two flipped surfaces will}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4518 \textcolor{comment}{ * not check to see if the physical flip has finished (i.e. will not return}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4519 \textcolor{comment}{ * DDERR\_WASSTILLDRAWING for that reason (but may for other reasons)).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4520 \textcolor{comment}{ * This allows an application to perform Flips at a higher frequency than the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4521 \textcolor{comment}{ * monitor refresh rate, but may introduce visible artifacts.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4522 \textcolor{comment}{ * Only effective if DDCAPS2\_FLIPNOVSYNC is set. If that bit is not set,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4523 \textcolor{comment}{ * DDFLIP\_NOVSYNC has no effect.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4524 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4525 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDFLIP\_NOVSYNC                       0x00000008L}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4526 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4527 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4528 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4529 \textcolor{comment}{ * Flip Interval Flags. These flags indicate how many vertical retraces to wait between}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4530 \textcolor{comment}{ * each flip. The default is one. DirectDraw will return DDERR\_WASSTILLDRAWING for each}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4531 \textcolor{comment}{ * surface involved in the flip until the specified number of vertical retraces has}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4532 \textcolor{comment}{ * ocurred. Only effective if DDCAPS2\_FLIPINTERVAL is set. If that bit is not set,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4533 \textcolor{comment}{ * DDFLIP\_INTERVALn has no effect.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4534 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4535 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4536 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4537 \textcolor{comment}{ * DirectDraw will flip on every other vertical sync}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4538 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4539 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDFLIP\_INTERVAL2                     0x02000000L}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4540 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4541 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4542 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4543 \textcolor{comment}{ * DirectDraw will flip on every third vertical sync}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4544 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4545 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDFLIP\_INTERVAL3                     0x03000000L}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4546 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4547 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4548 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4549 \textcolor{comment}{ * DirectDraw will flip on every fourth vertical sync}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4550 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4551 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDFLIP\_INTERVAL4                     0x04000000L}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4552 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4553 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4554 \textcolor{comment}{ * DirectDraw will flip and display a main stereo surface}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4555 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4556 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDFLIP\_STEREO                        0x00000010L}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4557 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4558 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4559 \textcolor{comment}{ * On IDirectDrawSurface7 and higher interfaces, the default is DDFLIP\_WAIT. If you wish}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4560 \textcolor{comment}{ * to override the default and use time when the accelerator is busy (as denoted by}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4561 \textcolor{comment}{ * the DDERR\_WASSTILLDRAWING return code) then use DDFLIP\_DONOTWAIT.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4562 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4563 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDFLIP\_DONOTWAIT                     0x00000020L}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4564 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4565 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4566 \textcolor{comment}{/****************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4567 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4568 \textcolor{comment}{ * DIRECTDRAW SURFACE OVERLAY FLAGS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4569 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4570 \textcolor{comment}{ ****************************************************************************/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4571 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4572 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4573 \textcolor{comment}{ * Use the alpha information in the pixel format or the alpha channel surface}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4574 \textcolor{comment}{ * attached to the destination surface as the alpha channel for the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4575 \textcolor{comment}{ * destination overlay.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{4682 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4683 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDOVER\_AUTOFLIP                         0x00100000l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4684 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4685 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4686 \textcolor{comment}{ * Display each field of video port data individually without}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4687 \textcolor{comment}{ * causing any jittery artifacts}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4688 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4689 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDOVER\_BOB                              0x00200000l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4690 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4691 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4692 \textcolor{comment}{ * Indicates that bob/weave decisions should not be overridden by other}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4693 \textcolor{comment}{ * interfaces.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4694 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4695 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDOVER\_OVERRIDEBOBWEAVE                 0x00400000l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4696 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4697 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4698 \textcolor{comment}{ * Indicates that the surface memory is composed of interleaved fields.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4699 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4700 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDOVER\_INTERLEAVED                      0x00800000l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4701 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4702 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4703 \textcolor{comment}{ * Indicates that bob will be performed using hardware rather than}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4704 \textcolor{comment}{ * software or emulated.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4705 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4706 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDOVER\_BOBHARDWARE                      0x01000000l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4707 }

\DoxyCodeLine{4710 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4711 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDOVER\_ARGBSCALEFACTORS                 0x02000000l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4712 }
