\DoxyCodeLine{4714 \textcolor{comment}{ * Indicates that ARGB scaling factors can be degraded to fit driver capabilities.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4715 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4716 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDOVER\_DEGRADEARGBSCALING               0x04000000l}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4717 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4718 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4719 \textcolor{comment}{/****************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4720 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4721 \textcolor{comment}{ * DIRECTDRAWSURFACE LOCK FLAGS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4722 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4723 \textcolor{comment}{ ****************************************************************************/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4724 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4725 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4726 \textcolor{comment}{ * The default.  Set to indicate that Lock should return a valid memory pointer}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4727 \textcolor{comment}{ * to the top of the specified rectangle.  If no rectangle is specified then a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4728 \textcolor{comment}{ * pointer to the top of the surface is returned.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4729 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4730 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDLOCK\_SURFACEMEMORYPTR                 0x00000000L     }\textcolor{comment}{// default}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4731 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4732 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4733 \textcolor{comment}{ * Set to indicate that Lock should wait until it can obtain a valid memory}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4734 \textcolor{comment}{ * pointer before returning.  If this bit is set, Lock will never return}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4735 \textcolor{comment}{ * DDERR\_WASSTILLDRAWING.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4736 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4737 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDLOCK\_WAIT                             0x00000001L}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4738 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4739 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4740 \textcolor{comment}{ * Set if an event handle is being passed to Lock.  Lock will trigger the event}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4741 \textcolor{comment}{ * when it can return the surface memory pointer requested.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4742 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4743 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDLOCK\_EVENT                            0x00000002L}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4744 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4745 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4746 \textcolor{comment}{ * Indicates that the surface being locked will only be read from.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4747 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4748 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDLOCK\_READONLY                         0x00000010L}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4749 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4750 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4751 \textcolor{comment}{ * Indicates that the surface being locked will only be written to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4752 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4753 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDLOCK\_WRITEONLY                        0x00000020L}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4754 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4755 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4756 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4757 \textcolor{comment}{ * Indicates that a system wide lock should not be taken when this surface}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4758 \textcolor{comment}{ * is locked. This has several advantages (cursor responsiveness, ability}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4759 \textcolor{comment}{ * to call more Windows functions, easier debugging) when locking video}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4760 \textcolor{comment}{ * memory surfaces. However, an application specifying this flag must}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4761 \textcolor{comment}{ * comply with a number of conditions documented in the help file.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4762 \textcolor{comment}{ * Furthermore, this flag cannot be specified when locking the primary.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4763 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4764 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDLOCK\_NOSYSLOCK                        0x00000800L}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4765 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4766 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4767 \textcolor{comment}{ * Used only with Direct3D Vertex Buffer Locks. Indicates that no vertices}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4768 \textcolor{comment}{ * that were referred to in Draw*PrimtiveVB calls since the start of the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4769 \textcolor{comment}{ * frame (or the last lock without this flag) will be modified during the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4770 \textcolor{comment}{ * lock. This can be useful when one is only appending data to the vertex}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4771 \textcolor{comment}{ * buffer}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4772 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4773 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDLOCK\_NOOVERWRITE                      0x00001000L}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4774 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4775 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4776 \textcolor{comment}{ * Indicates that no assumptions will be made about the contents of the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4777 \textcolor{comment}{ * surface or vertex buffer during this lock.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4778 \textcolor{comment}{ * This enables two things:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4779 \textcolor{comment}{ * -\/    Direct3D or the driver may provide an alternative memory}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4780 \textcolor{comment}{ *      area as the vertex buffer. This is useful when one plans to clear the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4781 \textcolor{comment}{ *      contents of the vertex buffer and fill in new data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4782 \textcolor{comment}{ * -\/    Drivers sometimes store surface data in a re-\/ordered format.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4783 \textcolor{comment}{ *      When the application locks the surface, the driver is forced to un-\/re-\/order}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4784 \textcolor{comment}{ *      the surface data before allowing the application to see the surface contents.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4785 \textcolor{comment}{ *      This flag is a hint to the driver that it can skip the un-\/re-\/ordering process}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4786 \textcolor{comment}{ *      since the application plans to overwrite every single pixel in the surface}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4787 \textcolor{comment}{ *      or locked rectangle (and so erase any un-\/re-\/ordered pixels anyway).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4788 \textcolor{comment}{ *      Applications should always set this flag when they intend to overwrite the entire}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4789 \textcolor{comment}{ *      surface or locked rectangle.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4790 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4791 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDLOCK\_DISCARDCONTENTS                  0x00002000L}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4792  \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4793 \textcolor{comment}{  * DDLOCK\_OKTOSWAP is an older, less informative name for DDLOCK\_DISCARDCONTENTS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4794 \textcolor{comment}{  */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4795 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDLOCK\_OKTOSWAP                         0x00002000L}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4796 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4797 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4798 \textcolor{comment}{ * On IDirectDrawSurface7 and higher interfaces, the default is DDLOCK\_WAIT. If you wish}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4799 \textcolor{comment}{ * to override the default and use time when the accelerator is busy (as denoted by}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4800 \textcolor{comment}{ * the DDERR\_WASSTILLDRAWING return code) then use DDLOCK\_DONOTWAIT.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4801 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4802 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDLOCK\_DONOTWAIT                        0x00004000L}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4803 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4804 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4805 \textcolor{comment}{ * This indicates volume texture lock with front and back specified.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4806 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4807 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDLOCK\_HASVOLUMETEXTUREBOXRECT          0x00008000L}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4808 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4809 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4810 \textcolor{comment}{ * This indicates that the driver should not update dirty rect information for this lock.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4811 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4812 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDLOCK\_NODIRTYUPDATE                    0x00010000L}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4813 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4814 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4815 \textcolor{comment}{/****************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4816 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4817 \textcolor{comment}{ * DIRECTDRAWSURFACE PAGELOCK FLAGS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4818 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4819 \textcolor{comment}{ ****************************************************************************/}}

\DoxyCodeLine{4848 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4849 \textcolor{comment}{ * Do this blt mirroring the surface left to right.  Spin the}}

\DoxyCodeLine{4851 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4852 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DDBLTFX\_MIRRORLEFTRIGHT                 0x00000002l}}
